 The comments apni aane vaali film 'bajrangi bhaijan' kii relies kaa intjaar kar rahe 49 saal ke salmaan ne kaha he ki lokapriy soshal netwarking plateform watsap par ek 'shararthpurna or jhootha' sandesh failaayaa ja rahaa he
 He has told his fans not to heed such rumors
 salmaan ne twit kiya, 'mere naam kaa istemaal karke dharm virdohi sandesh failaaye ja rahe hai, aise afvaahon par vishwaas nahin karen, ye bilkul bhi sach nahin he
 Police have been informed, they are taking action
 ' ' anti religious msg's doing the rounds using my name don't believe these rumors, not true at all informed the police, they r taking action
 — Salman Khan (@beingsalmankhan) July 11, 2015 iske saath hi unhone kaha, 'hameshaa sabhi dharmon kaa aadar kiya he
 
 
 All are under one roof in my house
 Always hv n vil respect all faiths arre have them all in my own house under 1 roof 
 - Salman Khan (@beingsalmankhan) July 11, 2015 'bajrangi Bhaijaan' directed by Kabir Khan also stars Kareena Kapoor and Nawazuddin Siddiqui
 film 17 july ko relies hogi
 The 49-year-old Salman, who is awaiting the release of his upcoming film 'bajrangi Bhaijaan', has said that a 'mischievous and false' message is being spread on the popular social networking platform whatsapp
 unhone apane prashansakon se kaha he ki ve aise afvaahon par dhyaan nahin den
 Salman tweeted, 'anti-religious messages are being spread using my name, don't believe such rumors, this is not true at all
 police ko suchit kar diya he, ve karrwai kar rahe hai
 '' anti religious msg's doing the rounds using my name don't believe these rumors, not true at all Informed the police, they r taking action

 Geeta Kapoor, the actress of the film Pakija, died at 9 a
m
 Saturday in an old age home in Mumbai
 kamaal amrohi kii film pakija main gita ne rajkumaar kii duusari patni kaa kirdaar nibhaayaa tha
 Producer Ashok Pandit has confirmed the news of Geeta's demise
 ashok ne apane twitor handle se ek video bhi share kiya he, gimen gita kaa shav najar aa rahaa he
 Billionaire's boss is Bobby Deol's wife, Aisi Hai Love Story Standing besides the dead body of actress # geetakapoor57 who was abandoned by her kids in # srvhospitala year back breathed her last at a suburban old age home today morning
 We tried our best to keep her healthy but her wait for her Son&daughter made her weaker day by day
 # rippic
 twitter
 com / ycchdzeset — Ashoke Pandit (@ashokepandit) May 26, 2018 Ashok wrote in his tweet - i am standing near the mortal body of 57-year-old Geeta Kapoor, whom her children had left in SRV hospital a year ago
 old age home main unhone aaj apni aakhri saans lee
 We tried hard to take care of them but their wait for son and daughter was making them weak every day
 nirahua kii maa ne poocha- itane paise kamaate ho, phir bhi fatty jeens pahante hoer body will be kept at Cooper Hospital Vileparle for two days hoping her Children to come and atleast do the last rites Otherwise We wl do our best to bid her a dignified good bye
 
 Thank u # drtripathisrv hospital@mumbaipolice # jivanashaoldhomefor being a great help

 com / zsh48xpg5a — Ashoke Pandit (@ashokepandit) May 26, 2018 According to a report, Ashok said - for the past one year she was waiting for her children, but no one came to meet them
 pichley shanivaar hamane unhen khush karne ke liye ek grand brakefast arange kiya tha
 She was fine but she was not happy
 kyonki vah apane bacchon ko dekhnaa chaahati thim
 Kareena Kapoor believes that her role in the movie 'heroine' is the boldest of the roles she has played so far
 karina ne kaha he ki kai sari abhinetriyaan is chunauteepurn bhoomika ko sweekaar nahin karti
 The director of this film Madhur Bhandarkar has said that the story of the film is based on real-life incidents of an actress from Hindi cinema
 karina ne bataaya, ‘main bachapan se hi abhinetri bananaa chaahati thi
 i am happy that 'heroine' has played one of the most challenging roles I've played
 kai sari abhinetri neeche girte superstar kii bhoomika par kaam nahin karnaa chaahati hai
 He said that usually you see the rise and fall of a star and then an uplifting career in films
 lekin 'heroin' main aap ek superstar ke girte kariyar ko dekhenge
 Kareena accepted the role because she is close to Mahi Arora's character and felt that the challenge was acceptable
 arjuna rampal, randeep hooda kii mukhya bhoomika vaali yah film 21 sitambar ko cinema gharon main pradarshit hone ja rahi he
 The film also stars Divya Dutta, Shahana Goswami and Ranveer Shorey in pivotal roles
 bhrashtachar ke khatme ko lekar bharat kii sthiti pehle se behatar hui he
 Transparency International has released Corruption Perception Index-2015 on corruption
 is suchi main shaamil 168 deshon main bharat ko 76waan sthaan diya gaya he
 India was ranked 85th in this list last year
 suchi main denmark pehle sthaan par bana hua he
 In a country with high scores, India's score in the Corruption Perceptions Index (CPI) 2015 remains 38, as in the previous year
 sipiai main 0 se lekar 100 tak ank hote hai
 The more points a country is given, the less corruption is in that country
 is maamle main denmark ko sabase zyada ank die gaye hai, vahaan sabase kam bhrashtachar he
 It is followed by Finland (90 points) and Sweden (89 points)
 report main is baar 168 deshon ko shaamil kiya gaya tha, jabaki 2014 kii report main 174 desh suchi main shaamil kiye gaye the
 The situation in Bhutan is better than India
 Based on the opinion of experts around the world, corruption in the government departments of countries in the CPI is estimated
 is maamle main bhutan 27wein paaydaan par he, or uski rank 65 he
 It is much better than India
 haalanki bharat ke duusare padosi deshon kii haalat kaaphi kharaab he
 China ranks 83 and Bangladesh 139 in the list
 vahiin pakistan, srilanka or nepal beete saalon kii tulana main thodaa sudhaar dekha gaya he
 North Korea and Somalia are at the bottom of the list, with eight points from both countries
 ugravadiyon ke hakkaani network se sambandh todane ke pakistan ke inkaar ke baad, ek pramukh america dainik ne kaha he ki samasyaon se jujh rahe desh kii sena america se madad lene or afgaan taliban ko sahyog dene kaa doharaa khel khel rahi he
 The New York Times has stated in an editorial titled "crippled, Chaotic Pakistan" that Pakistan has long been ignoring the Obama administration's request to take stern action against militants
 ye ugravadi seemaa paar kar, afghanistan main tainaat america balon par hamale karte hai
 It said that recently Taliban militants killed Pakistani soldiers by attacking from across the border and after this incident Islamabad should take that complaint seriously
 sampadakeey main kaha gaya he ‘‘charampanthiyon se mukaable kaa saajha aadhaar hona chahie lekin aisa nahin lagata ki pakistan ke sainya adhikari yah maanate hai
 They need to see that the militancy spread in Afghanistan is a threat to their country and thousands of Pakistani soldiers and civilians have fallen for it
 ’’ The New York Times has said, "however, they have refused to break ties with Haqqani and other militants while the militants are taking advantage of this situation and are also the biggest threat to America's efforts to stabilize the country
" 
 ’’ isamen kaha gaya he ki pakistan kaa raajnneetik tantra niskriy ho gaya he jabaki use seemaayi khatre se teji se nipatane kii jarurat he
 The editorial states that India's growing role matters as long as India's activities are transparent in Afghanistan and Indian companies are investing in war-torn countries
 akhbaar ne likhaa he ki pakistan varsh 2001 ke baad america kii sthiti kaa laabh uthaa saktaa tha jise afghanistan main alqaida or taliban ko haraane main madad kii jarurat he
 In this way Pakistan had the opportunity to grow into a more stable country
 pakistan ne arabon dollar kii madad bhi lee he
 "but his army is constantly playing a double game and the politicians are sitting silent
" ek ore america se dhan liya gaya or duusari ore afgaan taliban kii madad kii gai
 According to the editorial, "a large number of American troops will soon leave Afghanistan and Pakistan will find it difficult to defend against their enemies
" ’’tippaniyan The editorial further states that some members of the US Congress want to give the Haqqani network the status of a foreign terrorist organization, but such a step would not be right as it would pave the way for Pakistan to be given the status of a terrorist country and would have to face the ban
 tab usase sahyog milanaa mushkil ho jayega
 The newspaper wrote, "america has no other option but to try to work with Pakistan and its army
" ’’ aage likhaa he ki obama prashasan ke adhikariyon kaa dhairya kho rahaa he or america pakistan se dur nahin ho saktaa kyonki use afghanistan ke liye ahm aapurti maarg phir se kholane main tathaa taliban se shantivaarta main shaamil hone ke aagrah main uski madad kii jarurat he taaki varsh 2014 ke ant tak sainikon ko afghanistan se hataaya ja sake
 According to the newspaper, the US also needs to monitor Islamabad's growing nuclear weapons
 uske paas pakistan main ugravadiyon par drone hamale karte rahane ke alaava doosraa koi vikalp nahin he

 unhen yah dekhne kii jarurat he ki afghanistan main failaa ugravad khud unke desh ke liye khatra he or hajaaron pakistani sainik tathaa naagarik isaki bhent chadhe hai
 '' ‘neuyark times’ ne kaha he, ‘‘baharhaal, unhone hakkaani or anya ugravadiyon se sambandh todane se manaa kar diya he jabaki ugravadi is sthiti kaa phayda uthaa rahe hai or desh ko sthir karne ke america ke prayaason ke liye sabase bada khatra bhi hai
 "it says that Pakistan's political system has become dormant while it needs to deal with the border threat rapidly
" sampadakeey main kaha gaya he ki afghanistan main jab tak bharat kii gatividhiyaan paardarshee hai tab tak uski badhati bhoomika myne rakhti he or bhartiya companiyaan yuddh prabhavit desh main nivesh kar rahi hai
 The newspaper wrote that Pakistan could take advantage of the US situation after 2001 which needs help in defeating Al Qaeda and Taliban in Afghanistan
 is tarah pakistan ke paas ek adhik sthir desh ke rup main viksit hone kaa avasar tha
 Pakistan has also taken help of billions of dollars
 ‘‘lekin unki sena lagaataar doharaa khel khel rahi he tathaa raajnneetijna khamosh baithe hai
 On one hand, money was taken from the US and on the other side the Afghan Taliban was helped
 ’’ sampadakeey ke anusaar, ‘‘jald hi badi sankhya main america sainik afghanistan chhod denge or pakistan ko apane shatruon se bachaav karnaa mushkil ho jayega
 '' Comments sampadakeey main aage kaha gaya he ki america congress ke kuch sadsy hakkaani network ko videshi aatankwaadi sanghathan kaa darja dena chaahate hai lekin aisa kadam sahi nahin hoga kyonki isse pakistan ko aatankwaadi desh kaa darja dene kaa rasta ban jayega or use pratibandh kaa saamana karnaa hoga
 Then it will be difficult to cooperate with him
 akhbaar ne likhaa he, ‘‘america ke paas pakistan or uski sena ke saath kaam karne kii koshish ke alaava doosraa vikalp nahin he
 "it is further written that the Obama administration is losing the patience of the officials and the US cannot get away from Pakistan because it needs its help in reopening important supply routes to Afghanistan and urging the Taliban to join the peace talks
" So that by the end of 2014 the troops can be removed from Afghanistan
 akhbaar ke anusaar, america ko islamabad ke badhate parmaanu hathiyaaron kii nigaraanee karne kii bhi jarurat he
 It has no choice but to carry out drone attacks on militants in Pakistan

 vyavsaay se kismat or grahon kaa kya sambandh he?- har tarah ke vyavsaay or kaarobaar ke peeche kisi ek hi grah kii bhoomika hoti he- agar vah grah acha he to kaarobaar faltaa phulataa he- agar vah grah kamjor he to kaarobaar yaa to band ho jaataa he yaa nuksaan detaa he- kabhi kabhi kaarobaar kaa grah kisi grah ke kaaran gadabad ho jaataa he , aisi dasha main kaarobaar main utaar chadhaav chalata rahata he- kaarobaar se sambandhit grah ko majboot karke ham apane kaam ko kaaphi had tak behatar kar sakate hanvastron kaa vyavsaay- yah vyavsaay bahut saare grahon se sambandh rakhata he- parantu mukhya rup se yah shukr kaa vyavsaay he- is vyavsaay ko behatar karne ke liye nity praatah or saayam shukr ke mantra kaa jaap karen- ek sphatik kii maala gale main dhaaran karen- har shuukravaar ko maan lakshmi ko safed mithai kaa bhoga lagaaein- jahaan tak ho sake kaale rang ke prayog se bachenkhaane pine kii chizon kaa vyavsaay- anaaj kaa vyavsaay mukhya rup se brihaspati kaa vyavsaay he- pake hue bhojan ke peeche shukr kii bhoomika hoti he- jaleey khaadya ke peeche mukhya rup se chandramaa hota he- har tarah ke khaadya padaarth ke vyavsaay main safalataa ke liye shri krishna kii upasna karen- nity praatah or saayam "clin krishna clin" kaa 108 baar jaap karen- mastak par nity safed yaa pilaa chandan lagaaein- apane paas ek pile rang kaa reshmi rumal rakkhensaundarya prashaadhan yaa mahilaon se sambandhit vyavsaay- yah vyavsaay shuddh rup se shukr se sambandh rakhata he- kahin kahin par isamen chandramaa kii bhoomika bhi aa jaati he- is vyavsaay main safalataa ke liye apane kaarysthal par devi lakshmi kii sthapana karen- unhen nity praatah gulab kii sugandh kaa itr arpit karen- iske baad " shrin shriyai namah" kaa jaap karen- har shuukravaar shaam ko devi ko safed sugandhit phool arpit karanjameen, nirmaan, thekedaari aadi kaa vyavsaay- is vyavsaay kaa mukhya grah he - mangal- mangal kamjor hua to yah vyavsaay to duubataa hi he ,karje bhi chadh jate hai- is vyavsaay main safalataa ke liye laal rang ke hanuman ji kii sthapana karen- nity praatah unke saamne chameli ke tel kaa deepak jalaaen- iske baad bol bolkar ek baar hanuman chalisa kaa paath karen- mangalvaar ko mazdooron ko halava puri baantenshiksha, salaahkaarita kaa vyavsaay-- yah vyavsaay budh , brihaspati or shukr se sambandh rakhata he- parantu he mukhya rup se brihaspati kaa vyavsaay- is vyavsaay main safalataa ke liye bhagwaan shiv kii upasna kerani chahie- nity praatah shiv ji ko safed yaa pile phool chadhayen- iske baad " ashutoshay namah" kaa jaap karen- apane kaarysthal kaa rang halkaa pilaa yaa safed rakkhenlohe, koyale yaa petrol aadi kaa vyavsaay- yah vyavsaay shani or kuch had tak mangal kaa he- is vyavsaay main safalataa ke liye ek lohe kaa challa jarur dhaaran karen- dahini kalai main kaala reshmi dhaagaa baandhen yaa kaali strape vaali ghadi lagaaein- roj raat main 108 baar " shan shanaishcharai namah" kaa jaap karen- shanivaar ko tilyukt bhojan kaa daan karennaukari main safalataa paane ke upaay- agar aap naukari main safalataa chaahate hon to- ek lohe kaa challa, madhyamaa anguli main jarur dhaaran karen- har shanivaar ko pipal ke neeche sarson ke tel kaa deepak jarur jalaae If you are also fond of taking selfies, then through our article, we will inform you about which such smartphones are available in the Indian market which are equipped with 32 megapixel selfie camera

 palaayan kii sthiti un gaanv main he jo malkangiri se ekadam sate hue hai
 Hearing the news of the deaths of dozens of children in Malkangiri in Odisha from Japanese fever, the villagers are being shocked

 The people of Holler village on the outskirts of Chhattisgarh and Odisha are forced to flee

 graminon ne apane baccho ko apane rishtedaaro ke yahaan bhej diya he
